data-w=\"480\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_gif/icZklJrRfHgCsw1tPiaOtQnDiamSldfldicrG1BWtMicaYKHWIGocXkb14rD7k5duZxwAnIniboMXVrIH6xM1ia7t9GiaQ/640?wx_fmt=gif\"></section></section><section style=\"font-size: 12px;color: rgb(204, 204, 204);line-height: 2;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">脱毛奥义：稳准狠！（疼……</p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">其他的除毛方法，比如蜜蜡啊、拔毛啊……听起来就超疼的。很多脱毛膏用在身上也容易过敏，更别提私处这么敏感的部位了。激光脱毛倒是不怎么疼，但去美容院的话，光是比基尼区脱毛一次就要800块，而且还要做8次才能完全脱光，如果想要做全身，这价格真是令人吃不消……</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">于是，经过一番调查，我这个吃土少女发现了家用脱毛仪这个好东西！不仅比基尼区能用，而且<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(67, 161, 93);box-sizing: border-box;\">全身的毛毛都可以脱掉</span></strong>，不再长！</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(67, 161, 93);box-sizing: border-box;\">激光脱毛产生的光能，转化成热能，能直接作用于皮下的毛囊，让毛囊“不再工作”，也就可以达到长效脱毛的效果啦</span></strong>。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"margin-top: 10px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 100%;border-width: 0px 0px 0px 10px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(67, 161, 93);border-right-color: rgb(67, 161, 93);padding-left: 5px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"color: rgb(67, 161, 93);box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">我的脱毛仪初体验</strong></p></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">目前市面上的家用脱毛仪种类很多，而我完全是个新手，所以目标就是找一款不用太操心、手残党也能轻松上手的脱毛仪~</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(67, 161, 93);box-sizing: border-box;\">脱毛仪分为手动调档和自动调档两种</span></strong>。而调档调得准不准是直接关乎到脱毛效果的好坏的。因为我们人体身上每个部位的肤色不同，至少有4种以上不同的肤色，<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(67, 161, 93);box-sizing: border-box;\">脱毛时要用的光能量也就不一样，得随着肤色的不同去调整</span></strong>。<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(67, 161, 93);box-sizing: border-box;\">不然很容易会出现能量太高灼伤皮肤，或者是能量太低，脱毛无效的风险</span></strong>。想想看，去美容院还不是有专人按照你的肤色去调节脱毛光能量的大小吗？</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">所以，完全是小白的我很担心自己手动调档会出错。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">自动调档的脱毛仪也就成了我的首选。<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(67, 161, 93);box-sizing: border-box;\">可以智能识别肤色，直接自动调档</span></strong>，也就省去了上述可能发生的风险。经过一番调查，货比三家，我最终选择了<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(67, 161, 93);box-sizing: border-box;\">性价比最高</span></strong>的自动型脱毛仪，<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(67, 161, 93);box-sizing: border-box;\">博朗AI小闪电激光脱毛仪器PL3011</span></strong>。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.6666667\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/icZklJrRfHgCsw1tPiaOtQnDiamSldfldicrklQcvWFbH4lzjUmjjH4QyKXib1elibHX5fpwaPAUyY5wibxkLNSSPkcBQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">博朗作为<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(67, 161, 93);box-sizing: border-box;\">德国大品牌</span></strong>，质量值得信赖，在小姐姐们非常精致爱美的日本，<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(67, 161, 93);box-sizing: border-box;\">销量也是No.1</span></strong>。此外，<span style=\"color: rgb(6, 6, 6);box-sizing: border-box;\">博朗<span style=\"color: rgb(52, 52, 52);box-sizing: border-box;\">小闪电还获得了</span></span><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(67, 161, 93);box-sizing: border-box;\">美国FDA和欧洲皮肤健康联盟的双重权威认证，</span></strong><span style=\"color: rgb(52, 52, 52);box-sizing: border-box;\">在众多脱毛仪中</span><span style=\"color: rgb(6, 6, 6);box-sizing: border-box;\">，</span><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(67, 161, 93);box-sizing: border-box;\">只有小闪电获得了欧洲皮肤健康联盟的认证。</span></strong>护舒宝卫生巾也有这个认证，比基尼区也可安心用。因此小闪电的安全性直击我心，很心水它在脱毛的同时不伤害皮肤。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">事不宜迟，到手就开始用！一打开包装，发现里面还附赠了一把刮毛刀。读了使用说明之后，<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(67, 161, 93);box-sizing: border-box;\">发现是需要先用刮毛刀把毛刮掉，然后再用脱毛仪。</span></strong>激光脱毛的靶组织是毛囊中的黑色素，如果不把毛发刮干净，毛会和毛囊中的黑色素竞争吸收激光能量，影响脱毛效果，同时还会增加疼痛感。没有刮除的毛发吸收光能量后还可能使毛发烧焦，引起表皮损伤，出现灼伤、红肿等不良现象。<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(67, 161, 93);box-sizing: border-box;\">所以用脱毛仪前大家记得先刮干净皮肤表面的毛发，然后可以适当抹一些芦荟胶或者身体乳进行脱毛前的保湿工作。</span></strong></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">我选的这款小闪电是香芋紫色，很漂亮~这配色和质感十分可爱，差不多像iPhone的大小，握在手里也感觉很舒服。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br 93);box-sizing: border-box;\">AI智能识别肤色，每秒高达80次，还能根据肤色的不同自动换档，反应很灵敏，不需要手动调节，也就不会面临被灼伤的风险</span></strong>，简直完全就是为我这种手残党+仪器小白量身打造的。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">把脱毛仪垂直抵在皮肤上，按下小按钮，自动识别肤色后，侧面的灯就会亮起——<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(67, 161, 93);box-sizing: border-box;\">肤色越白，灯亮得越多，输出的能量也就越高，完全不用自己去调整档位。</span></strong>脱毛简直不要太方便，就算是新手也能一次上手，再也不用担心因为操作复杂会将脱毛仪闲置在家了。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">然后大按钮可以调节是<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(67, 161, 93);box-sizing: border-box;\">点按模式还是滑动模式</span></strong>，可以单独一下一下按，也可以长按在皮肤上直接滑动。如果是胳膊腿的话，长按滑动就好，<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(67, 161, 93);box-sizing: border-box;\">滑到哪脱到哪儿</span></strong>~出光十分快速，全程下来大概也就3首歌的时间就能脱完全身，真的是手残党的福音了，脱完毛记得也要擦一些身体乳做做保湿的工作。</p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.5631579\" data-type=\"gif\" data-w=\"380\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_gif/icZklJrRfHgCsw1tPiaOtQnDiamSldfldicrw1jpu1hTpe1P14Ix17TBfcFUt67uFMEz2wdiaPpX11FVt5toSBTsMcw/640?wx_fmt=gif\"></section></section><section style=\"font-size: 12px;color: rgb(204, 204, 204);line-height: 2;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.5625\" data-type=\"gif\" data-w=\"400\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: style=\"font-size: 12px;color: rgb(204, 204, 204);line-height: 2;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">滑动模式，滑到哪里脱哪里</p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">这款脱毛仪一共有<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(67, 161, 93);box-sizing: border-box;\">日常和轻柔两种模式</span></strong>。日常模式适合日常护理，用在胳膊腿上啊之类的；轻柔模式适合初次使用或敏感部位，比如比基尼区或唇部。是的，我这个人，连唇毛都是需要脱的，以前我都是用刮眉刀……</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">按下小的按钮，灯亮起是轻柔模式，灯熄灭就是日常模式。我感觉自己还是个挺怕疼的人，<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(67, 161, 93);box-sizing: border-box;\">闪光的一瞬间会有一点热感。</span></strong>轻柔模式用在四肢时是很轻微的温热和像叮咬的感觉，在腋下会稍微强一点点。日常模式的话，其实我自己的感觉是并没有比轻柔模式明显更疼……所以总得来说两种模式的痛感都是可以接受的~</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">姐妹们不要觉得痛感很可怕，<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(67, 161, 93);box-sizing: border-box;\">稍微感觉有点疼才说明脱毛仪起到了效果，如果完全没感觉，那估计毛也脱不掉了</span></strong>……白费功夫。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">另外，我虽然只用了一次，但发现脱毛仪脱过的部位毛发真的是连根脱掉的，而用刮毛刀的部分在两天过后就已经长出短短的毛了~<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(67, 161, 93);box-sizing: border-box;\">脱完毛后还有意外惊喜：皮肤看起来变白了更光滑了，连毛孔都被隐匿了。</span></strong></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: 12:53:50","title":"脖子痛？简单三步有效预防 | 果断练","link":"http://weixin.sogou.com/weixin?type=2&query=%E6%9E%9C%E5%A3%B3%E7%BD%91+%E8%84%96%E5%AD%90%E7%97%9B%EF%BC%9F%E7%AE%80%E5%8D%95%E4%B8%89%E6%AD%A5%E6%9C%89%E6%95%88%E9%A2%84%E9%98%B2%C2%A0%7C%C2%A0%E6%9E%9C%E6%96%AD%E7%BB%83","description":"<div><div><div id=\"media\" class=\"rich_media_thumb_wrp\">\n\n            <img class=\"rich_media_thumb\" class=\"rich_media_content\" id=\"js_content\">\n                    \n\n                    \n\n                    \n                    \n                    <section style=\"display: none;\" data-tools=\"新媒体管家\" data-label=\"powered by xmt.cn\"><br></section><section style=\"color: rgb(52, 52, 52);line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 16px;\"><section style=\"letter-spacing: 0px;padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">一天到晚低头盯着手机和显示器，你的脖子还好吗？</span><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">如果总是坐着工作，可以做一下这个测试，得分能预测未来1年会不会脖子疼[1]：</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span></p></section><section style=\"padding-left: 19px;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"width: 0px;margin-top: 2em;margin-right: 22px;margin-left: -19px;display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"width: 0px;border-right: 20px solid rgb(228, 239, 230);border-top: 10px solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 10px solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><section style=\"line-height: 0;width: 0px;\"><svg viewbox=\"0 0 1 1\" style=\"vertical-align:top;\"></svg></section></section><section style=\"width: 0px;margin-top: -19px;margin-bottom: -19px;margin-left: 3px;border-right: 18px solid rgb(228, 239, 230);box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;border-top: 9px solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 9px solid transparent !important;\"><section style=\"line-height: 0;width: 0px;\"><svg viewbox=\"0 0 1 1\" style=\"vertical-align:top;\"></svg></section></section></section><section style=\"padding: 10px;width: 100%;margin-top: -2em;min-height: 4em;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(228, 239, 230);box-shadow: rgba(255, 185, 149, 0) -2px 2px 5px;background-color: rgb(228, 239, 230);box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"font-size: 14px;color: rgb(88, 89, 89);line-height: 2;padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">回答符合下列描述的频率，记录每个问题的得分（从不=0分，很少=1分，有时=2分，经常=3分，总是=4分）：</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">1. 工作时坐姿如下图；</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">2. 除了午休，工作中还可以间断休息；</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">3. 即使出现颈部疼痛，还是可以继续坐着工作；</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">4. 工作中出现颈痛时，会用颈部前屈、后伸或左右侧屈来缓解症状；</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">5. 拉伸颈部肌肉；</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">6. 做加强颈部肌肉力量和耐力的练习。</p></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.4232862\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"919\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/icZklJrRfHgD7VmIeXfqFQpDriarhcuqNZEdN8WtG2eSIWAB5bN602RNK9OVuqeDwEzcOelsMEmv0TIjAjmyG4xw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"font-size: 12px;line-height: 1.4;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box;\">颈部竖直、背部挺直地靠在椅背上 | 参考文献[1]</span></p></section><section style=\"letter-spacing: 0px;padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">6项得分相加为测试总分（0~24分），总分越高越好，如果低于9分，1年内出现颈部疼痛的可能是88.1%；总分低于6分的话，几乎可以肯定颈痛将会找上门来。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span></p></section><section style=\"margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding-right: 6px;padding-bottom: 6px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"padding-top: 6px;display: inline-block;background-color: rgb(237, 242, 238);box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: -6px;margin-bottom: -6px;margin-left: 6px;background-color: rgb(67, 161, 93);color: rgb(255, 255, 255);padding-right: 6px;padding-left: 6px;font-size: 20px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">坐“正”不能靠别人，</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">要自己找到感觉</p></section></section></section><section style=\"letter-spacing: 0px;padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">得分很低也不用慌，把问题中的第1、5、6项变成“总是”，就可以明显减小颈痛的可能[2-5]。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">第1项说起来最简单，找个人站在侧面指点，很快就能摆成正确坐姿。不过几分钟之后，多数人都会变回驼背伸头的样子。依靠其他人提醒不是办法，<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">只有自己找到坐正的感觉，才能随时随地调整好。</strong></span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">躺着比坐着更容易摆正身体，先从仰卧姿势开始找“正”的感觉。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span></p></section><section style=\"padding-right: 20px;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;padding: 10px;vertical-align: top;width: 100%;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(255, 185, 149, 0);box-shadow: rgba(255, 185, 149, 0) 3px 3px 5px;background-color: rgb(218, 238, 242);margin-right: -20px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"font-size: 14px;color: rgb(88, 89, 89);line-height: 2;padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">下面的练习仅针对健康人，患相关疾病者请遵从医生的建议。特别是颈痛伴有头晕、视物不清、肢体无力、感觉异常、发热等症状者。</p></section></section><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 0px;margin-top: 2em;margin-left: 19px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"width: 0px;border-left: 20px solid rgba(255, 185, 149, 0);border-top: 10px solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 10px solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><section style=\"line-height: 0;width: 0px;\"><svg viewbox=\"0 0 1 1\" style=\"vertical-align:top;\"></svg></section></section><section style=\"width: 0px;margin-top: -19px;margin-bottom: -19px;border-left: 18px solid rgb(218, 238, 242);box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;border-top: 9px solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 9px solid transparent !important;\"><section style=\"line-height: 0;width: 0px;\"><svg viewbox=\"0 0 1 1\" style=\"vertical-align:top;\"></svg></section></section></section></section><section style=\"letter-spacing: 0px;padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.5256917\" data-type=\"gif\" data-w=\"253\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_gif/icZklJrRfHgD7VmIeXfqFQpDriarhcuqNZWAbuO4C57P5Zn4JOQbdYK9s28weoTkyU2IhpVT0HMVmdCT7Dnoic22w/640?wx_fmt=gif\"></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;font-size: 12px;line-height: 1.4;color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">躺在枕头上，让额头与下巴连线、耳屏与脖子连线都基本平行地面，脚踩地；腰背部前屈、后伸，找到中间位置（躯干拉到最长）并维持住丨作者供图</p></section><section style=\"letter-spacing: 0px;padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.5433071\" data-type=\"gif\" data-w=\"254\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; display: inline; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_gif/icZklJrRfHgD7VmIeXfqFQpDriarhcuqNZhsUEu3ziaLT0sBWH4U823zcOf6UrrJUEfzVGhhrBvoSurLyFx2XLBBA/640?wx_fmt=gif\"></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;font-size: 12px;line-height: 1.4;color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">在这个姿势下，舌头顶上颚，嘴唇合拢，牙齿稍分开；把下巴拉向地面（挤出双下巴），拉长颈部，同时避免颈部前侧肌肉用力而突出（手触摸位置）丨作者供图</p></section><section style=\"letter-spacing: 0px;padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.5335968\" data-type=\"gif\" data-w=\"253\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; display: inline; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_gif/icZklJrRfHgD7VmIeXfqFQpDriarhcuqNZjvoQHT9RGmzkf7O3w4QeiaffZUDHh0A5sWKccpqPEDzT4Jftfc4Tw0w/640?wx_fmt=gif\"></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;font-size: 12px;line-height: 1.4;color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">不要出现下巴扬起或头抬起的错误动作丨作者供图</p></section><section style=\"letter-spacing: 0px;padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">这种躯干和颈部被拉长的感觉，通常代表身体是“正”的。熟悉之后，试着在坐姿和站姿下重复“正”的感觉，对着镜子确认自己的姿态，并牢牢记住[6, 7]。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.5567376\" data-type=\"gif\" data-w=\"282\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_gif/icZklJrRfHgD7VmIeXfqFQpDriarhcuqNZCqJuichxdrnEA9nMrtia9zxGbDLS1FpNycFVIPP392dUacAZEYverBkw/640?wx_fmt=gif\"></section></section><section style=\"line-height: 1.4;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box;\">站立时摆正姿势丨作者供图</span></p></section><section style=\"letter-spacing: 0px;padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding-right: 6px;padding-bottom: 6px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"padding-top: 6px;display: inline-block;background-color: rgb(237, 242, 238);box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: -6px;margin-bottom: -6px;margin-left: 6px;background-color: rgb(67, 161, 93);color: rgb(255, 255, 255);padding-right: 6px;padding-left: 6px;font-size: 20px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">预防，从最常用的姿势开始</p></section></section></section><section style=\"letter-spacing: 0px;padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">找到“正”的感觉之后，无论用什么姿势做什么事，都尽量保持这种感觉[8]。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">每天维持时间最长的姿势，通常是测试中的第1项——坐在桌前盯着显示器。除了维持上面的姿势，靠在椅背上时，尽量让显示器与眼睛高度相近，胳膊支撑在椅子扶手或桌面上。如果有条件多站起来活动，提高第2项的得分，当然更好。（详见<a href=\"https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MTg1MjI3MzY2MQ==&amp;mid=2651724581&amp;idx=1&amp;sn=9fd3f0c569a9a903e5960492fa96efd5&amp;chksm=5da23fb76ad5b6a190b38f3894fc9de8b58c1a08af4b5f26f81c41ca4a7c1c045e3e08e58c65&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect\" target=\"_blank\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" data-linktype=\"2\">《科学久坐指南》</a>）</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">用时第二长的是睡眠。无论仰卧还是侧卧，都保证枕头高度让头颈与脊柱在一条直线上。（详见<a href=\"https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MTg1MjI3MzY2MQ==&amp;mid=2651725039&amp;idx=1&amp;sn=b7e8be3d9c51b54289c838a9381f38d1&amp;chksm=5da2387d6ad5b16b68c405584f5cc7632c34d4aebc954b54d8c7b58fe5353b51c76a73d80b52&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect\" target=\"_blank\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" data-linktype=\"2\">《如何科学地躺着玩儿手机》</a>）</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">另外，每天用手机的时间也很长。无论站、坐或躺，看手机的时候都别低着头。打电话的时候，不要把手机夹在耳朵和肩之间，如果通话时间长，最好使用耳机或免提功能。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">除了调整姿势，戒烟、减少肩负或手提重物也能帮助减少颈痛[9]。坐车时系好安全带并避免在车上睡觉，可以减少急刹车对颈部的损伤。最后，不要接受非专业人员提供的肩颈按摩，否则可能因手法不当或过重而损伤颈部[10]。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span></p></section><section style=\"margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding-right: 6px;padding-bottom: 6px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"padding-top: 6px;display: inline-block;background-color: rgb(237, 242, 238);box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: -6px;margin-bottom: -6px;margin-left: 6px;background-color: rgb(67, 161, 93);color: rgb(255, 255, 255);padding-right: 6px;padding-left: 6px;font-size: 20px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">拉伸紧张的肌肉</p></section></section></section><section style=\"letter-spacing: 0px;padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">感觉对的姿势太累，保持不住？可能是久坐和运动少，让颈部肌肉有的太紧，有的太松，变得不平衡。<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">测试中的第5项拉伸颈部可以放松过紧的肌肉，帮助身体回到正常位置</strong>[11]。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">下面的每个动作重复10次，每天做两组（可以在颈部不舒服的时候做），每周至少练习5天，能帮助减少颈痛[6, 7, 12]。做所有动作之前都需要把头颈摆正，缓慢拉伸到有牵拉感觉后保持10秒，不要猛地用力。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.4216028\" data-type=\"gif\" data-w=\"287\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; display: inline; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_gif/icZklJrRfHgD7VmIeXfqFQpDriarhcuqNZdsBNVkKWWSffkFH51Vicx54M62Mh9EM9wicj8FkbPR6xUnQIlAHJoia1A/640?wx_fmt=gif\"></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;font-size: 12px;line-height: 1.4;color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">1. 前屈后伸-下巴靠近胸，然后头靠近背；2. 侧屈-头向左侧屈的同时把右肩向下沉，换另一侧；3. 旋转-保持视线平行地面，头向左或向右旋转丨作者供图</p></section><section style=\"letter-spacing: 0px;padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.4201389\" data-type=\"gif\" data-w=\"288\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_gif/icZklJrRfHgD7VmIeXfqFQpDriarhcuqNZfzTicfNnCvpheicF9my1x5mEZ55B9DrAjrBsEJWGVrMySRCFKicxk9NQA/640?wx_fmt=gif\"></section></section><section style=\"font-size: 12px;line-height: 1.4;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box;\">侧屈时耸肩，无法充分拉伸肌肉丨作者供图</span></p></section><section style=\"letter-spacing: 0px;padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.4285714\" data-type=\"gif\" data-w=\"287\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; display: inline; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_gif/icZklJrRfHgD7VmIeXfqFQpDriarhcuqNZslaYRnCxv5Cl0yHN7wDrAKibzyuoSKSlbe78TYBRA3HVpv8yibZAADjg/640?wx_fmt=gif\"></section></section><section style=\"font-size: 12px;line-height: 1.4;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box;\">左手触左肩，尽力让大臂贴近耳朵，头稍向右转并低头，换另一侧丨作者供图</span></p></section><section style=\"letter-spacing: 0px;padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.55625\" data-type=\"gif\" data-w=\"320\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_gif/icZklJrRfHgD7VmIeXfqFQpDriarhcuqNZEYJ3yq9bDNCoxLX0ozszPmWHhF8bTxWLvGWnaMqt4neOria16FL0j7A/640?wx_fmt=gif\"></section></section><section style=\"font-size: 12px;line-height: 1.4;color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;\">左脚在前跨立，右大臂平行地面，小臂抵住固定物，重心前压，拉伸胸肩部</span><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">丨作者供图</span></p></section><section style=\"letter-spacing: 0px;padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding-right: 6px;padding-bottom: 6px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"padding-top: 6px;display: inline-block;background-color: rgb(237, 242, 238);box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: -6px;margin-bottom: -6px;margin-left: 6px;background-color: rgb(67, 161, 93);color: rgb(255, 255, 255);padding-right: 6px;padding-left: 6px;font-size: 20px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">加强无力的肌肉</p></section></section></section><section style=\"letter-spacing: 0px;padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">放松之后，还需要完成最后一项——加强力量弱的肌肉，才能轻松保持健康姿势。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">说到练力量，很多人期望通过用力仰头来纠正平时低头、弯着脖子的姿势。其实，<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">头前伸的不良姿态比低头更难改变，颈痛预防中最需要练习的是后缩下巴的肌肉</strong>[13-18]。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">先用文章开头的仰卧姿势找到下巴后缩、颈部拉长的感觉，然后坐起来练习。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.430605\" data-type=\"gif\" data-w=\"281\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; display: inline; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_gif/icZklJrRfHgD7VmIeXfqFQpDriarhcuqNZ88ic8qnjib079rrfHjl1Hwpo7qibgibbmC7iapM94ZEMiavLbp0hOfIzWasg/640?wx_fmt=gif\"></section></section><section style=\"font-size: 12px;line-height: 1.4;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box;\">双手放在头后，尽力把下巴水平向后缩，抵抗双手的力，维持10秒，休息10秒，重复10~15次丨作者供图</span></p></section><section style=\"letter-spacing: 0px;padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.4121622\" data-type=\"gif\" data-w=\"296\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; display: inline; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_gif/icZklJrRfHgD7VmIeXfqFQpDriarhcuqNZ213jugGwwiaqWQMAoZV6I4O6bx06O47x5jbVMgXLvuFrFsl6acQEzibg/640?wx_fmt=gif\"></section></section><section style=\"font-size: 12px;line-height: 1.4;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box;\">手放得过低或过高，练不到期望加强的肌肉丨作者供图</span></p></section><section style=\"letter-spacing: 0px;padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">除了缩下巴，还可以加入其他动作，让颈部在各个方向上都更加稳定[7]。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.4109589\" data-type=\"gif\" data-w=\"292\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; display: inline; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_gif/icZklJrRfHgD7VmIeXfqFQpDriarhcuqNZrlrFTbZYpPOePCIqX2Wibe61OopB5IHicHgibemxtnXdafbp59HkQINcw/640?wx_fmt=gif\"></section></section><section style=\"font-size: 12px;line-height: 1.4;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box;\">1. 双手放在前额，用头抵抗手的力量；2. 右手放在右脸颊，头向右侧屈，换另一侧；3. 右手放在右耳后，头向右旋转，换另一侧丨作者供图</span></p></section><section style=\"letter-spacing: 0px;padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">所有动作做完后，记得重复一下颈前屈、后伸、侧屈、旋转的拉伸动作，放松一下肌肉。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">如果加入肩部力量和稳定性训练，预防颈痛的效果更好，不过那属于另一个话题了[7]。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">除了针对局部的动作，全身运动也有减轻颈痛的效果，比如快走、跑步、游泳等有氧运动，以及瑜伽等[11, 19, 20]。不过，尽量不要选择需要用力抬头、低头或头颈部容易受到冲撞的运动[8]。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">看到这里，回想一下刚才测试的得分，是时候逐条把“从不”变成“总是”了。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"> </span></p></section><section style=\"margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: flex;align-items: center;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"flex: 1 1 auto;height: 1px;background-color: rgb(204, 204, 204);box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><br></section><section style=\"flex: 0 1 auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section
